dcl_color v2
dcl_position o0
dcl_texcoord o1.xyz
dcl_texcoord1 o2.xyz
dcl_color o3
dcl_texcoord2 o4.xyz
dcl_texcoord3 o5
dcl_texcoord5 o6

add r1, -r0.x, c16
dp4 r0.y, c9, v0
add r2, -r0.y, c17

mad r3.xyz, c11, v1.x, r3
mad r3.xyz, c13, v1.z, r3

mad r1, r3, r3, r2

rsq r2.y, r1.y
rsq r2.z, r1.z
rsq r2.w, r1.w

mad r1, r1, c19, r3.y
mul r0, r0, r2
max r0, r0, c24.x
rcp r2.x, r1.x
rcp r2.y, r1.y
rcp r2.z, r1.z
rcp r2.w, r1.w
mul r0, r0, r2
mul r1.xyz, r0.y, c1
mad r1.xyz, c0, r0.x, r1
mad r0.xyz, c2, r0.z, r1
mad r0.xyz, c3, r0.w, r0
mul r0.w, r4.y, r4.y
mad r0.w, r4.x, r4.x, -r0.w
mul r1, r4.yzzx, r4.xyzz
mov o1.xyz, r4
dp4 r2.x, c20, r1
dp4 r2.y, c21, r1
dp4 r2.z, c22, r1
mad r1.xyz, c23, r0.w, r2
add o4.xyz, r0, r1
dp4 r0.y, c5, v0

dp4 r0.w, c7, v0
